<font color = white>&#34;I&#39;m takin&#39; that blade from ya&#39;, one way, <b><i>OR ANOTHER..!&#34;</font>, he spoke as he sprung himself forward.

His hands facing the earth as he flipped over for a kick to the head. Matching his allies kick to the knees in the form of a </i>combination hit.<i> 

|| C Striking, C- Damage | 1/3 DT used ||</font></font></font>
